class="_accordion-icon_1wnp5_28"></div></summary></details><div id="content-5743473921055" class="_visibility-precluded_1wnp5_147 _content_1wnp5_94 accordion_content-container__QJe_F"><div class="rich-text_component_frame__PqAAF"><h4 class="_text-heading-xl-max-medium_z017j_58 _text-heading-xl-min-medium-max-large_z017j_132 _text-heading-xl-min-large_z017j_206 text-ND900 stacked_standard-content-remaining___CirG"><section id="2Wge86lpfp8LdyLZsrIUSk" data-content="componentngaccordion" data-reducedlist="accordion" data-testid="reduced-list-frame"><section style="--disclosure-border:#0000001f;--disclosure-icon:currentColor" class="accordion_exterior-configuration__k9exI" data-testid="disclosure"><details name="_S_6_" class="_details_1wnp5_14"><summary aria-details="9762471240406" data-amp-id="what-is-the-hims-weight" data-amp-title="What is the Hims Weight Loss Membership? " data-amp-event="ACCORDION:[details.open]"><span data-testid="disclosure-label" class="accordion_heading-container__4ZYx_"><p class="_text-label-m-max-medium_z017j_34 _text-label-m-min-medium-max-large_z017j_108 _text-label-m-min-large_z017j_182 font-medium text-ND900">What is the Hims Weight Loss Membership? </p></span><div class="_accordion-icon_1wnp5_28"></div></summary></details><div id="content-9762471240406" class="_visibility-precluded_1wnp5_147 _content_1wnp5_94 accordion_content-container__QJe_F"><div role="definition" id="9762471240406" class="_interior_1wnp5_114"><p class="_text-body-s-max-medium_z017j_10 _text-body-s-min-medium-max-large_z017j_84 _text-body-s-min-large_z017j_158 text-ND600 text-margin-healthy">The Hims Weight Loss Membership gives you access to a range of GLP-1 medications if eligible, plus unlimited support from a dedicated Care Team.

Your membership also includes in-app weight tracking to help you monitor your progress, dosage adjustments as your needs evolve, and support for managing common side effects.</p></div></div><details name="_S_6_" class="_details_1wnp5_14"><summary aria-details="6747809387475" data-amp-id="how-much-does-the-hims" data-amp-title="How much does the Hims Weight Loss Membership cost?" data-amp-event="ACCORDION:[details.open]"><span data-testid="disclosure-label" class="accordion_heading-container__4ZYx_"><p class="_text-label-m-max-medium_z017j_34 _text-label-m-min-medium-max-large_z017j_108 _text-label-m-min-large_z017j_182 font-medium text-ND900">How much does the Hims Weight Loss Membership cost?</p></span><div class="_accordion-icon_1wnp5_28"></div></summary></details><div id="content-6747809387475" class="_visibility-precluded_1wnp5_147 _content_1wnp5_94 accordion_content-container__QJe_F"><div role="definition" id="6747809387475" class="_interior_1wnp5_114"><p class="_text-body-s-max-medium_z017j_10 _text-body-s-min-medium-max-large_z017j_84 _text-body-s-min-large_z017j_158 text-ND600 text-margin-healthy">You’ll pay a $39 membership fee at checkout for your first month. After that, your membership auto-renews at $149 per month (medication cost not included). You can cancel anytime, but canceling your membership will also cancel any active medication plan and access to care through the platform.</p><p class="_text-body-s-max-medium_z017j_10 _text-body-s-min-medium-max-large_z017j_84 _text-body-s-min-large_z017j_158 text-ND600 text-margin-healthy">If prescribed, your medication is billed separately (monthly or upfront, based on your plan), and the price of the medication depends on your prescribed treatment, if eligible. You can cancel your medication plan anytime, and it won’t affect your active membership.</p></div></div><details name="_S_6_" class="_details_1wnp5_14"><summary aria-details="7044610982966" data-amp-id="what-are-my-medication-options" data-amp-title="What are my medication options through Hims?" data-amp-event="ACCORDION:[details.open]"><span data-testid="disclosure-label" class="accordion_heading-container__4ZYx_"><p class="_text-label-m-max-medium_z017j_34 _text-label-m-min-medium-max-large_z017j_108 _text-label-m-min-large_z017j_182 font-medium text-ND900">What are my medication options through Hims?</p></span><div class="_accordion-icon_1wnp5_28"></div></summary></details><div id="content-7044610982966" class="_visibility-precluded_1wnp5_147 _content_1wnp5_94 accordion_content-container__QJe_F"><div role="definition" id="7044610982966" class="_interior_1wnp5_114"><p class="_text-body-s-max-medium_z017j_10 _text-body-s-min-medium-max-large_z017j_84 _text-body-s-min-large_z017j_158 text-ND600 text-margin-healthy">Hims offers access to an affordable range of FDA-approved GLP-1 medications, including the Wegovy<sup>®</sup> Pill, Wegovy<sup>®</sup> Pen, Zepbound<sup>®</sup> KwikPen<sup>®</sup>, Zepbound<sup>®</sup> Vial, Foundayo™ Pill, and Ozempic<sup>®</sup> Pill.</p><p class="_text-body-s-max-medium_z017j_10 _text-body-s-min-medium-max-large_z017j_84 _text-body-s-min-large_z017j_158 text-ND600 text-margin-healthy">Designed to fit your lifestyle and your wallet, these medications are clinically proven to promote weight loss or are prescribed for it in off-label use.</p><div class="options_embed-entry-block_embed-frame__cQeTm" data-embed="componentngdisclaimer"><div data-content="componentngdisclaimer" id="5NAo87Jl85Y4zouvSxeOQi" class="disclaimer_frame__D6Efi" data-testid="disclaimer-frame"><p data-testid="disc-paragraph" class="_text-label-s-max-medium_z017j_30 _text-label-s-min-medium-max-large_z017j_104 _text-label-s-min-large_z017j_178 text-ND500 text-margin-healthy"><span data-readmore-target="true">Ozempic</span><sup><span data-readmore-target="true">®</span></sup><span data-readmore-target="true"> and Wegovy</span><sup><span data-readmore-target="true">®</span></sup><span data-readmore-target="true"> are the registered trademarks of Novo Nordisk A/S. Zepbound</span><sup><span data-readmore-target="true">®</span></sup><span data-readmore-target="true"> and KwikPen</span><sup><span data-readmore-target="true">®</span></sup><span data-readmore-target="true"> are registered trademarks of Eli Lilly and Company. Foundayo</span><sup><span data-readmore-target="true">™</span></sup><span data-readmore-target="true"> is a trademark of Eli Lilly and Company. Hims, Inc. is not affiliated with or endorsed by Eli Lilly and Company.</span></p></div></div></div></div><details name="_S_6_" class="_details_1wnp5_14"><summary aria-details="5274965229727" data-amp-id="are-video-visits-with-a" data-amp-title="Are video visits with a doctor required?" data-amp-event="ACCORDION:[details.open]"><span data-testid="disclosure-label" class="accordion_heading-container__4ZYx_"><p class="_text-label-m-max-medium_z017j_34 _text-label-m-min-medium-max-large_z017j_108 _text-label-m-min-large_z017j_182 font-medium text-ND900">Are video visits with a doctor required?</p></span><div class="_accordion-icon_1wnp5_28"></div></summary></details><div id="content-5274965229727" class="_visibility-precluded_1wnp5_147 _content_1wnp5_94 accordion_content-container__QJe_F"><div role="definition" id="5274965229727" class="_interior_1wnp5_114"><p class="_text-body-s-max-medium_z017j_10 _text-body-s-min-medium-max-large_z017j_84 _text-body-s-min-large_z017j_158 text-ND600 text-margin-healthy">Depending on your state, treatment may be determined without a video visit. If a visit is needed, scheduling a video or audio appointment is simple and convenient. If prescribed, a provider will be just a message away for follow-ups, adjustments, and ongoing support. Response times may vary.</p></div></div><details name="_S_6_" class="_details_1wnp5_14"><summary aria-details="6712304744056" data-amp-id="is-insurance-required" data-amp-title="Is insurance required?" data-amp-event="ACCORDION:[details.open]"><span data-testid="disclosure-label" class="accordion_heading-container__4ZYx_"><p class="_text-label-m-max-medium_z017j_34 _text-label-m-min-medium-max-large_z017j_108 _text-label-m-min-large_z017j_182 font-medium text-ND900">Is insurance required?</p></span><div class="_accordion-icon_1wnp5_28"></div></summary></details><div id="content-6712304744056" class="_visibility-precluded_1wnp5_147 _content_1wnp5_94 accordion_content-container__QJe_F"><div role="definition" id="6712304744056" class="_interior_1wnp5_114"><p class="_text-body-s-max-medium_z017j_10 _text-body-s-min-medium-max-large_z017j_84 _text-body-s-min-large_z017j_158 text-ND600 text-margin-healthy">Insurance isn’t required, so there are no complicated insurance questions or health insurance plan considerations.</p></div></div><details name="_S_6_" class="_details_1wnp5_14"><summary aria-details="5567497915633" data-amp-id="who-qualifies-for-weight-loss" data-amp-title="Who qualifies for weight loss medication at Hims?" data-amp-event="ACCORDION:[details.open]"><span data-testid="disclosure-label" class="accordion_heading-container__4ZYx_"><p class="_text-label-m-max-medium_z017j_34 _text-label-m-min-medium-max-large_z017j_108 _text-label-m-min-large_z017j_182 font-medium text-ND900">Who qualifies for weight loss medication at Hims?</p></span><div class="_accordion-icon_1wnp5_28"></div></summary></details><div id="content-5567497915633" class="_visibility-precluded_1wnp5_147 _content_1wnp5_94 accordion_content-container__QJe_F"><div role="definition" id="5567497915633" class="_interior_1wnp5_114"><p class="_text-body-s-max-medium_z017j_10 _text-body-s-min-medium-max-large_z017j_84 _text-body-s-min-large_z017j_158 text-ND600 text-margin-healthy">A state-licensed provider reviews the health history, weight loss goals, and unique patient needs of every individual patient to see if they qualify before prescribing any kind of treatment.</p></div></div><details name="_S_6_" class="_details_1wnp5_14"><summary aria-details="16884687429544" data-amp-id="are-glp-1-s-available-in-all" data-amp-title="Are GLP-1s available in all states?" data-amp-event="ACCORDION:[details.open]"><span data-testid="disclosure-label" class="accordion_heading-container__4ZYx_"><p class="_text-label-m-max-medium_z017j_34 _text-label-m-min-medium-max-large_z017j_108 _text-label-m-min-large_z017j_182 font-medium text-ND900">Are GLP-1s available in all states?</p></span><div class="_accordion-icon_1wnp5_28"></div></summary></details><div id="content-16884687429544" class="_visibility-precluded_1wnp5_147 _content_1wnp5_94 accordion_content-container__QJe_F"><div role="definition" id="16884687429544" class="_interior_1wnp5_114"><p class="_text-body-s-max-medium_z017j_10 _text-body-s-min-medium-max-large_z017j_84 _text-body-s-min-large_z017j_158 text-ND600 text-margin-healthy">GLP-1s are not yet available in all 50 states. However, Hims is working to expand our offering as soon as possible.</p></div></div><details name="_S_6_" class="_details_1wnp5_14"><summary aria-details="16919683933725" data-amp-id="how-long-do-i-need" data-amp-title="How long do I need to stay on medication?" data-amp-event="ACCORDION:[details.open]"><span data-testid="disclosure-label" class="accordion_heading-container__4ZYx_"><p class="_text-label-m-max-medium_z017j_34 _text-label-m-min-medium-max-large_z017j_108 _text-label-m-min-large_z017j_182 font-medium text-ND900">How long do I need to stay on medication?</p></span><div class="_accordion-icon_1wnp5_28"></div></summary></details><div id="content-16919683933725" class="_visibility-precluded_1wnp5_147 _content_1wnp5_94 accordion_content-container__QJe_F"><div role="definition" id="16919683933725" class="_interior_1wnp5_114"><p class="_text-body-s-max-medium_z017j_10 _text-body-s-min-medium-max-large_z017j_84 _text-body-s-min-large_z017j_158 text-ND600 text-margin-healthy">Weight loss treatment is meant for long-term use. When you stop taking it, the triggers that previously drove unhealthy eating behaviors may return. Always speak with a licensed medical provider before stopping treatment.</p></div></div><details name="_S_6_" class="_details_1wnp5_14"><summary aria-details="7835662871704" data-amp-id="when-will-i-see-weight" data-amp-title="When will I see weight loss results?" data-amp-event="ACCORDION:[details.open]"><span data-testid="disclosure-label" class="accordion_heading-container__4ZYx_"><p class="_text-label-m-max-medium_z017j_34 _text-label-m-min-medium-max-large_z017j_108 _text-label-m-min-large_z017j_182 font-medium text-ND900">When will I see weight loss results?</p></span><div class="_accordion-icon_1wnp5_28"></div></summary></details><div id="content-7835662871704" class="_visibility-precluded_1wnp5_147 _content_1wnp5_94 accordion_content-container__QJe_F"><div role="definition" id="7835662871704" class="_interior_1wnp5_114"><p class="_text-body-s-max-medium_z017j_10 _text-body-s-min-medium-max-large_z017j_84 _text-body-s-min-large_z017j_158 text-ND600 text-margin-healthy">Remember, results aren’t instant. Because everyone’s weight loss journey is different, the timeline for results may vary from person to person.
</p></div></div><details name="_S_6_" class="_details_1wnp5_14"><summary aria-details="9468317701448" data-amp-id="can-a-provider-change-my" data-amp-title="Can a provider change my dosage at any point during my treatment?" data-amp-event="ACCORDION:[details.open]"><span data-testid="disclosure-label" class="accordion_heading-container__4ZYx_"><p class="_text-label-m-max-medium_z017j_34 _text-label-m-min-medium-max-large_z017j_108 _text-label-m-min-large_z017j_182 font-medium text-ND900">Can a provider change my dosage at any point during my treatment?</p></span><div class="_accordion-icon_1wnp5_28"></div></summary></details><div id="content-9468317701448" class="_visibility-precluded_1wnp5_147 _content_1wnp5_94 accordion_content-container__QJe_F"><div role="definition" id="9468317701448" class="_interior_1wnp5_114"><p class="_text-body-s-max-medium_z017j_10 _text-body-s-min-medium-max-large_z017j_84 _text-body-s-min-large_z017j_158 text-ND600 text-margin-healthy">Hims members receiving weight loss medications can request a medication adjustment right from the app.</p><p class="_text-body-s-max-medium_z017j_10 _text-body-s-min-medium-max-large_z017j_84 _text-body-s-min-large_z017j_158 text-ND600 text-margin-healthy">If a provider determines a dosage change is necessary, they’ll write a new prescription and provide you with updated treatment information.</p><p class="_text-body-s-max-medium_z017j_10 _text-body-s-min-medium-max-large_z017j_84 _text-body-s-min-large_z017j_158 text-ND600 text-margin-healthy">Dosage and titration vary based on provider discretion. Pricing may vary by dosage.</p><p class="_text-body-s-max-medium_z017j_10 _text-body-s-min-medium-max-large_z017j_84 _text-body-s-min-large_z017j_158 text-ND600 text-margin-healthy">
</p></div></div></section></section></div></section></article></main><footer class="_footer_13xxf_2 _set-footer-text-color-default_k2duq_2 global-footer_component_footer-negative-shift-selector__yWHWW" style="--footer-bg:#000000;--footer-bg-secondary:#ffffff1c;--footer-bg-tertiary:#ffffff12;--footer-text:#ffffff;--footer-text-recessive:#ffffff82;--footer-text-invert:#000000e3;--footer-logo:#ffffff2b" data-brand="hims" data-testid="footer" data-top-barbg="black" data-tracking-prefix="footer"><section class="_disclaimers_13xxf_74 _set-footer-text-color-recessive_k2duq_6 _bind-to-container-on-large-up_13xxf_23" data-testid="footer-disclaimers"><div class="_disclaimer_13xxf_74"><div data-content="componentngdisclaimer" id="1dS8NvjPP8XBqMbuY1FJpV" class="disclaimer_frame__D6Efi" data-testid="disclaimer-frame"><p data-testid="disc-paragraph" class="_text-label-s-max-medium_z017j_30 _text-label-s-min-medium-max-large_z017j_104 _text-label-s-min-large_z017j_178 text-ND500 text-margin-healthy"><span data-readmore-target="true">Zepbound</span><sup><span data-readmore-target="true">®</span></sup><span data-readmore-target="true"> and Foundayo</span><sup><span data-readmore-target="true">™</span></sup><span data-readmore-target="true"> are FDA approved for weight loss. Zepbound</span><sup><span data-readmore-target="true">®</span></sup><span data-readmore-target="true"> and KwikPen</span><sup><span data-readmore-target="true">®</span></sup><span data-readmore-target="true"> are registered trademarks, and Foundayo™ is a trademark of Eli Lilly and Company.
